msg:We stayed here for our family of five on our Chinese New Year trip.
We stayed in the Presidential Suite, the largest room type, as we were staying with my wife and three children.
When we entered the room, we were amazed at how spacious it was... There were two bedrooms, both of which were very large with double beds. Not only was there a large living room and dining room, but there were also three toilets, two shower rooms, and a bathtub, making it feel like a luxury apar**ent.
We requested a room with a good view, and from our room on the top floor we could see the venue used for the Asian Games, the illuminated skyscrapers, and even the Chinese New Year fireworks. We could walk to the canal, which has a beautiful night view, but there were not many restaurants nearby. The breakfast buffet seemed to have a small selection of items...
The staff were very kind and helpful to us, even though we didn't speak Chinese, so we had no particular concerns.
The room was well cleaned and we had a very pleasant time.

msg:The summer heat in Jiangxiang is still mild, and there are evening orioles in the garden on a sunny day. â€”â€”"Early Summer" by Lu You of the Song Dynasty
The rain is coming, and the thunder is new last night. â€”â€”Xu Ji, Song Dynasty
"Early Summer" If the beauty of spring lies in the blooming of hundreds of flowers, then the beauty of early summer lies in the blooming of all kinds of flowers. Early summer is quiet and beautiful, and everything is budding and full of life. In such a beautiful season, because of the exhibition, we reunited with Hangzhou International Expo Center Beichen Hotel.

The hotel is located in the Hangzhou International Expo Center complex. You can walk to the Expo Center through a passage on the second floor.

The hotel has complete facilities, including a lobby bar, sky garden, book bar, lounge, and gym. After work, you can choose your own way of leisure. The room is relatively spacious and has a wide view, with a clear view of the rows of tall buildings outside.

There are also a variety of breakfast varieties, many of which are Jiangnan cuisine, which are delicious and provide enough nutrition for the day.

The service is attentive and enthusiastic. Especially the young lady named Dai at the front desk, another young lady who was on duty with her on the night of check-in, and the concierge brother Gao Xiaoyu. They are very dedicated and enthusiastic to answer guests' questions and provide assistance to guests as much as possible.

The hotel is relatively close to Hangzhou East Railway Station and Hangzhou Xiaoshan Airport. It is an ideal hotel for business and family travel.
